<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aengeven</i>. <ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hand, to pass

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenhalen</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenhouden</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arrest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hail (a cab); to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> (someone in order to ask a question)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep up, to keep on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>Voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:normale.html>normale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gloeilamp.html>gloeilamp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beste.html>beste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:compromis.html>compromis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:temperatuur.html>temperatuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> ca. 2500 <a href = vnd.unilang:graden.html>graden</a> Celsius <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangehouden.html>aangehouden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">For a normal lightbulb, as the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> compromise a <a href = vnd.unilang:temperaturen.html>temperature</a> of ca. 2500 degrees Celsius <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>kept up</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be ongoing, to persist</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep on, to continue wearing (clothing)</li>

***aankleden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aankleden.html>aankleden</a> (4994)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenclêden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleden.html>kleden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aankleden.html>aankleden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress, put clothing on someone or something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welke.html>Welke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idioot.html>idioot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangekleed.html>aangekleed</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What idiot <b>put <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> on</b> the cat?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get dressed, put <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> on oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haastig.html>Haastig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleedde.html>kleedde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zodra.html>zodra</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorde.html>hoorde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naderen.html>naderen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Hastily he <b>got dressed</b> as soon as he <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> someone approaching.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to furnish with textile, furniture, decorations etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergt.html>vergt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:smaak.html>smaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fraaie.html>fraaie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stijlvol.html>stijlvol</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleden.html>kleden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> good taste to <b>furnish</b> a nice room stylishly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress up, present with embellishments, <a href = vnd.unilang:excuses.html>excuses</a> etc.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aankondiging.html>aankondiging</a> (11107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aankondigen.html>aankondigen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aankondiging.html>aankondiging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aankondigingen.html>aankondigingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aankondiging.html>aankondiginkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***aanleggen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanleggen.html>aanleggen</a> (10584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenleggen</i>. </p>
